Captain's Log — Sunday 19 July 2026. We travelled to Borstal CC.

We won the toss and I elected to bat — the right call, I felt.
Our innings came to 169/1 from 20 overs. Hannah Odling 33 not out did the bulk of the scoring, ably supported by Nicola Coomansingh 31 not out, Claire Daniels 28 not out. The extras column added a handy 41.
Then it was our turn with the ball. The opposition made 109/6 from 20 overs. Bethany Baker 33 not out top-scored. We sent Faith Rogers, Rosie Coyle back without troubling the scorers. 🦆 We leaked 34 in extras, which won't do. Laura Thorogood led the attack with 2-4. Also among the wickets: Carly Copping (2-19) and Ashleigh Bland (1-33).
I chipped in with 27.
For the season charts, Hannah Odling leads the 2026 Women's Softball run charts with 295 runs; Carly Copping sits 2nd in the 2026 Women's Softball wicket charts with 8 wickets.
A fine win by 60 runs. Onwards. 🏏
